  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,

  `slug` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('select','color','text') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'select',

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `imageable_type` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `imageable_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `file_name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `file_path` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `thumbnail_small` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `thumbnail_medium` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_optimized` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `original_size` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_size` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `mime_type` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `width` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `height` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `alt_text` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `order` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `is_primary` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `dominant_color` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `color_palette` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin DEFAULT NULL CHECK (json_valid(`color_palette`)),
  `original_extension` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `correct_extension` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `metadata` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin DEFAULT NULL CHECK (json_valid(`metadata`)),
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `stock_after` decimal(12,4) NOT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `inventory_reservations`
--

CREATE TABLE `inventory_reservations` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `order_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `order_item_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `material_variant_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `source_type` enum('product','extra') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'product' COMMENT 'Origen de la reserva: product o extra',
  `source_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ID del producto o extra que genera la reserva',
  `quantity` decimal(14,4) NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('reserved','released','consumed') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'reserved',
  `created_by` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `consumed_by` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `consumed_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `released_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `orders`
--

CREATE TABLE `orders` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `order_parent_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `related_order_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `uuid` char(36) NOT NULL,
  `order_number` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `cliente_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `client_measurement_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `design_export_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('draft','confirmed','in_production','ready','delivered','cancelled') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'draft',
  `urgency_level` enum('normal','urgente','express') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'normal',
  `priority` tinyint(3) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 50,
  `payment_status` enum('pending','partial','paid') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  `subtotal` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `discount` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `requires_invoice` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `iva_amount` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `total` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `amount_paid` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `balance` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `materials_cost_snapshot` decimal(15,4) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Costo de materiales al iniciar produccion - INMUTABLE',
  `total_stitches_snapshot` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Puntadas totales al iniciar producción',
  `embroidery_cost_snapshot` decimal(10,4) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Costo de bordado = puntadas/1000 × tarifa',
  `cost_per_thousand_snapshot` decimal(10,4) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Tarifa por millar usada en el cálculo',
  `promised_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `minimum_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `delivered_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `notes` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_by` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_by` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `created_by` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `order_items`
--

CREATE TABLE `order_items` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `uuid` char(36) NOT NULL,
  `order_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `product_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `product_variant_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `product_type_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `requires_measurements` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `client_measurement_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `measurements` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Medidas capturadas inline para este ítem específico' CHECK (json_valid(`measurements`)),
  `measurement_history_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `product_name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `variant_sku` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `unit_price` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL,
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  `subtotal` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL,
  `discount` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `total` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL,
  `estimated_extras_cost` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.00,
  `real_extras_cost` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `embroidery_text` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `customization_notes` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `personalization_type` enum('none','text','measurements','design') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'none',
  `design_approved` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `design_approved_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `design_approved_by` bigint(20) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `design_file` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `design_original_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `design_status` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  `design_notes` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `custom_text` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_multiplier_snapshot` decimal(4,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1.00,
  `estimated_lead_time` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `measurements_hash_at_approval` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_annex` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `annexed_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('pending','in_progress','completed','cancelled') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  `has_pending_adjustments` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `final_total` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `product_materials`
--

CREATE TABLE `product_materials` (
  `id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `product_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `material_variant_id` bigint(20) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `quantity` decimal(12,4) NOT NULL,
  `active_for_variants` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Array of Variant UUIDs/IDs this material applies to. NULL = Global.' CHECK (json_valid(`active_for_variants`)),
  `unit_cost` decimal(14,4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0000,
  `total_cost` decimal(14,4) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (`quantity` * `unit_cost`) STORED,
  `is_primary` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `notes` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL

--
-- Índices para tablas volcadas
--

--
-- Indices de la tabla `activity_logs`
--
ALTER TABLE `activity_logs`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD UNIQUE KEY `activity_logs_uuid_unique` (`uuid`),
  ADD KEY `activity_logs_user_id_index` (`user_id`),
  ADD KEY `activity_logs_action_index` (`action`),
  ADD KEY `activity_logs_model_type_index` (`model_type`),
  ADD KEY `activity_logs_model_type_model_id_index` (`model_type`,`model_id`),
  ADD KEY `activity_logs_created_at_index` (`created_at`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `application_types`
--
ALTER TABLE `application_types`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD UNIQUE KEY `application_types_slug_unique` (`slug`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `attributes`
--
ALTER TABLE `attributes`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD UNIQUE KEY `attributes_slug_unique` (`slug`),
  ADD KEY `attributes_slug_index` (`slug`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `attribute_values`
--
ALTER TABLE `attribute_values`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD KEY `attribute_values_attribute_id_index` (`attribute_id`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `cache`
--
ALTER TABLE `cache`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`key`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `cache_locks`
--
ALTER TABLE `cache_locks`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`key`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `categories`
--
ALTER TABLE `categories`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD UNIQUE KEY `categories_slug_unique` (`slug`),
  ADD KEY `categories_slug_index` (`slug`),
  ADD KEY `categories_parent_id_index` (`parent_id`),
  ADD KEY `categories_is_active_index` (`is_active`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `category_design`
--
ALTER TABLE `category_design`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD UNIQUE KEY `category_design_category_id_design_id_unique` (`category_id`,`design_id`),
  ADD KEY `category_design_design_id_index` (`design_id`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `category_unit`
--
ALTER TABLE `category_unit`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD UNIQUE KEY `category_unit_material_category_id_unit_id_unique` (`material_category_id`,`unit_id`),
  ADD KEY `category_unit_unit_id_foreign` (`unit_id`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `clientes`
--
ALTER TABLE `clientes`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD KEY `clientes_estado_id_foreign` (`estado_id`),
  ADD KEY `clientes_recomendacion_id_foreign` (`recomendacion_id`);

--
-- Indices de la tabla `client_measurements`
--
ALTER TABLE `client_measurements`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  ADD UNIQUE KEY `client_measurements_uuid_unique` (`uuid`),
